Friendly and pleasant staff. I'd recommend reservations, online. Indoor and outdoor seating are available, beautiful atmosphere.
They have a nice wine and cocktail selection but no blender drinks.
The menu has a nice selection and our meals (Steak and Lobster) were prepared by Chef Lacy,
the medium rare fillet was perfect through out. Risotto was so flavorful and the mushrooms perfectly.
Chef Lacy was very cordial and enhanced my meal experience with a personal visit at the table.
Enjoyable live music was relaxing.  The overal ambiance was family friendly, quiet and private.< /Review>

< Review>
First visit to this restaurant. I was with my husband and my parents.  Aesthetically, it looks nice. There was a maitre'd at the door. He was welcoming, but I didn't understand the point of the tuxedo when there weren't tablecloths on the tables. Is this supposed to be a "fine dining" establishment? There wasn't even a wine list. The room had 3 4-tops, 1 table was set up for a party of 6, and there was already a group of 9 seated, waiting for their dinner. There was also a bar-type table along the walk that seated 4.  The menu had something for everyone. The wait for our entrees was VERY long. It was a good thing we got a small plate of focaccia, 1 piece for each of us, but it took about 45 minutes before we were served. I had the short ribs. Though tender, the meat was stringy and dry. The risotto was okay. My dad ordered a burger but we had to send it back because it was undercooked.  When it came the second time, it still had a part that was undercooked, but we didn't want to bother with it anymore. My dad stated that In & Out had a better burger that what he had.  I really wanted to like this place, but I don't think I'll be returning.</Review>

< Review>
You haven't had a real sandwich until you eat here.

I am so cautious about eating tuna salad anywhere.  Their tuna has chopped onions and celery and it's perfectly seasoned.  So good!

Their tomato soup tasted so fresh and yummy. Perfect for dipping your sandwich.

The ambiance and furniture are so amazing. They have a patio with a fire pit and water features.  If you're in the waiting area, they even have heated fans on the ceiling.

Best soup, salad and sandwich spot in town.</Review>

My girlfriend and I recently dined here. Upon arrival, the door was immediately opened for us by Mark, who was our waiter. Mark's attitude, as well as his mannerisms, were exceptional. We were quickly seated at our table. My girlfriend ordered the Salmon, which was very well cooked and delicious. < Text>
What a truly amazing experience I had at Periodontics of the Desert.  Thank you to the entire staff and especially Dr. Warshawsky.  After a failed root canal by different practitioner, due to an unidentified underlying condition I found myself at risk of losing my tooth.  I was referred to Periodontics of the Desert to address the underlying condition and attempt to save the tooth.  I was seen immediately due to the time sensitivity surrounding the probability of a successful outcome (saving my tooth!)  After a consultation visit in which a detailed path forward was laid out for me we set a procedure date for that same week.  Talk about terrified. This was going to be the most significant procedure I had ever experienced.  Dr. Warshawsky took the time to address each and everyone of my fears.  He was very clear in setting my expectation level.  We were 50/50 at best to save my tooth.

On the day of the procedure the staff did an amazing job at keeping me calm and making me comfortable.  Not only was the procedure a complete success (I woke up with my tooth still in my mouth!!) it was truly a piece of cake.  No pain or soreness immediately following the surgery and the recovery was equally easy.  I was given a very clear set of guidelines for healing success that proved to be perfect.

Thanks again to everyone at Periodontics of the Desert for getting me through this challenging experience as best possible.  I would strongly recommend Dr. Warshawsky and his team if you find yourself in the unfortunate need of periodontal work.< /Text>

I took driving sessions and the drive test with Navjot sir.

Navjot sir is punctual and provides a flexible schedule.

The session time is usually confirmed a day prior to the practice, since he has to consider the availability of multiple students and give priority to those whose drive tests are approaching.

What I particularly liked about the sessions:

1) Does not prompt a lot, mostly to provide directions. Allows the student to make small mistakes and points them out, so that we can learn from it. This practice instills an awareness of the road conditions in the student and an understanding of the corrective actions to be taken.

2) The routes taken during the practice sessions present different scenarios that reinforce the driving guidelines given in the DMV handbook.

I am glad to share that I passed the driving test with very few errors.

Would highly recommend driving sessions with Navjot sir / A One Driving Center< /Review>

<UserId.>112288326715490339524</UserId.><Name>Ni Phi</Name><Time>1486414340793</Time><rating>4<//rating>< text>
Given its a recycling and trash dump, it's not soo bad. When it's hot it can smell a bit but not too over powering, although I hate the bee's and fly's. Driving inside the place can get scary and you can get blocked in by big trucks if you go right before closing (there's a massive line that goes thruout parking lot which is smaller and they are parked pretty much.). It could be a lot worse overall but also could be better. I think they pay a little more than the 3rd party centers at the grocery stores so I keep coming back here and just follow a few rules of mine and it works out fine for me. Suggestions: wear a pair of old tennis shoes (no flip flops gross), bring disposable gloves to wear, hand sanitizer and some kind of wipe sanitizer disposable type thing, if can avoid the heat do it (go earlier in the AM or if I can wait till weather cools I do), have stuff separated before you go there, and take at least a big trash bag full of smashed cans and one of plastics which is all I recycle here otherwise I feel it's not worth the whole trip if I'm not cashing in at least $30. Sunscreen for those fair skinned like I am. Oh and on hot days when the bees and bugs are flying all around, a face mask to protect your mouth and you don't have to worry about one flying in.< /text>

I'm not a person who had gone to a Dentist unless it was necessary. After having moved from Ojai to Camarillo, I found myself with a cracked tooth and in need of immediate assistance. The office staff are friendly, and Dr. Pez is wonderful. She put me at ease, and even tailored the dosage of the numbing medication to help me cope with it better (I typically get anxious and nearly pass out).

I've been back many times since then, and each time has been just as good as the last.  I was fitted for a night guard to help me with my aggressive (VERY aggressive) grinding, and after I chewed through the first guard, Dr. Pez and crew were kind enough to get me set up with a new one that was stronger.

With their help, my tooth sensitivity has drastically declined, and my teeth are in better shape than they've been in in years. The office is also fairly modern in how it keeps contact with you, and I enjoy getting the emails and text reminders for appointments.

I would recommend this office to anyone, and especially someone with a bit of Dental anxiety. Everyone there has been just great.< /Review>

<user_id>113990318691182536268<//user_id>< user_name>
Shruffle< /user_name>
<date>1414114815250</date><Rate>3<//Rate>< Review>
Went to Czubiak for 13 years. Everything is great as far as friendliness, and I love Dr. Czubiak personally, but I am going to write an honest review. Nice man, not so good at doing dental work. For example, I have a front tooth that is chipped, and since 1981 the repairs have always lasted at least 10 or more years. The material eventually wears down, or falls off. Czubiak fixed this chip 4 times in 13 years, and when smoothing with the drill he hits my other front tooth constantly. In a magnifying mirror the material is jagged, and I expect it to fall off soon again. The fix is always a huge disappointment, and I don't know why I was so lazy that I didn't look for another dentist to do this repair years ago. Another example, I had 3 inlays done, and the drilling is hard and aggressive, and 2 years later I still have some pain in those teeth. Michael doesn't encourage you to do work you don't need, but he doesn't stop you either, and explain things like - the life of a tooth, why you don't want to drill it more than necessary, because you will need a root canal. The kind of information a patient needs to make an informed decision for their mouth health. The cleanings and scaling were just ok also. Last but not least, after 13 years of devoted business, I needed a special prescription that after years of knowing a patient's individual health concerns, should not have been a problem for Dr. Czubiak to prescribe. He flat out refused, saying he felt "uncomfortable", which left me high and dry, and with ultra-sensitive tooth pain. My physician who I have only seen less than 3 times, had no problem writing me a prescription for this "substance" once I explained why I needed it. I was deeply hurt that I couldn't rely on my own dentist for help I needed when he has known me long enough to feel "comfortable" with supporting what I need. That is the entire reason you try and stay with one dentist for so long! So they get to know your individual needs. I can't write what this "substance" is, or he will know who I am. Being friendly is wonderful, but you have to be able to provide excellent dentistry too, and honestly Michael just doesn't do this, and he may let you down when you really need his help. If you need things like root canals, he refers out for this too. Suffice it to say, there are a lot of great dentists out there that are not only just as funny and friendly, but do excellent dentistry work, including things like root canals. Look elsewhere.

P.S. Lisa at the front, who also left a review here, is part of what makes people want to come back. She is so calming. Also tried the female dentist here once, and she hit a nerve when she injected me. Her fault? No, but still an unpleasant experience of pain. Never tried Shapiro, but I am finally done with this office, and off to one with an exceptionally talented hand at dentistry. Good luck Michael.< /Review>
